if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '40a0f5111cf799c80e10fe39aa049c19763553e0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '40a0f5111cf799c80e10fe39aa049c19763553e0') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '66e8325cbc063eacfe314974b94f04d73a7ced7d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '40a0f5111cf799c80e10fe39aa049c19763553e0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php') != 'ed62e875517a1c8c17b7d742c782d394b814ce51') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php') !== 'ed62e875517a1c8c17b7d742c782d394b814ce51') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php') !== 'e0812d03257295543e1753b90c6dfcaf2dc6b9cd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php') !== 'ed62e875517a1c8c17b7d742c782d394b814ce51') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/095_attachments/OIDplusPagePublicAttachments.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 614\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 614') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
